	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '59e0ab95e22a764e6fad4b82bc557ed93e78ed9c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '59e0ab95e22a764e6fad4b82bc557ed93e78ed9c') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '59e0ab95e22a764e6fad4b82bc557ed93e78ed9c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}

			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php') !== '2acf8bfb36782fb2d9ec81ada50cc0e424ad89e1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/800_plugins/OIDplusPageAdminPlugins.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	writefile_25();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') != 'cc11de9d98d75ea392b5b243a7180920ef11a1d1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== 'cc11de9d98d75ea392b5b243a7180920ef11a1d1') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '710a65b6fddd8f1429d41328458e047395ab9d1f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_25();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== 'cc11de9d98d75ea392b5b243a7180920ef11a1d1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
		}
	}
